1	package main
2	
3	import (
4		"fmt"
5		"os"
6	
7		"github.com/spf13/cobra"
8	
9		"github.com/saigyo/cc-what-have-i-done/internal/discovery"
10		"github.com/saigyo/cc-what-have-i-done/internal/tui"
11	)
12	
13	// options holds all CLI flag values.
14	type options struct {
15		session          string
16		project          string
17		latest           bool
18		out              string
19		title            string
20		includeSubagents bool
21		noRedact         bool
22		force            bool
23		open             bool
24	}
25	
26	func newRootCmd() *cobra.Command {
27		opts := &options{}
28		cmd := &cobra.Command{
29			Use:   "ccwhid",
30			Short: "Turn a Claude Code session transcript into a browsable HTML report",
31			Long: "ccwhid (cc-what-have-i-done) renders a Claude Code session " +
32				"transcript into a self-contained static HTML report. Run with no " +
33				"flags to browse sessions in an interactive TUI.",
34			SilenceUsage: true,
35			RunE: func(cmd *cobra.Command, args []string) error {
36				return run(cmd, opts)
37			},
38		}
39		f := cmd.Flags()
40		f.StringVar(&opts.session, "session", "", "session id or unambiguous prefix to render")
41		f.StringVar(&opts.project, "project", "", "project path or name to scope to")
42		f.BoolVar(&opts.latest, "latest", false, "render the most recent session")
43		f.StringVar(&opts.out, "out", "", "output directory (default ./ccwhid-report/<session-short>)")
44		f.StringVar(&opts.title, "title", "", "override the report title")
45		f.BoolVar(&opts.includeSubagents, "include-subagents", true, "include subagent (Task) activity")
46		f.BoolVar(&opts.noRedact, "no-redact", false, "disable secret redaction")
47		f.BoolVar(&opts.force, "force", false, "overwrite a non-empty output directory")
48		f.BoolVar(&opts.open, "open", false, "open the report in a browser when done")
49		return cmd
50	}
51	
52	func run(cmd *cobra.Command, opts *options) error {
53		root, err := discovery.DefaultRoot()
54		if err != nil {
55			return err
56		}
57		si, needTUI, err := resolveSession(opts, root)
58		if err != nil {
59			return err
60		}
61		if needTUI {
62			groups, err := discovery.Scan(root)
63			if err != nil {
64				return err
65			}
66			sel, err := tui.Run(groups)
67			if err != nil {
68				return err
69			}
70			if sel.Canceled {
71				fmt.Fprintln(cmd.OutOrStdout(), "canceled")
72				return nil
73			}
74			si = sel.Session
75			opts.includeSubagents = sel.IncludeSubagents
76			opts.noRedact = !sel.Redact
77			opts.open = sel.Open
78			if sel.OutDir != "" {
79				opts.out = sel.OutDir
80			}
81		}
82		outDir, err := generate(opts, si)
83		if err != nil {
84			return err
85		}
86		fmt.Fprintf(cmd.OutOrStdout(), "report written to %s\n", outDir)
87		if opts.open {
88			if err := openInBrowser(outDir); err != nil {
89				fmt.Fprintf(cmd.ErrOrStderr(), "warning: could not open browser: %v\n", err)
90			}
91		}
92		return nil
93	}
94	
95	func main() {
96		if err := newRootCmd().Execute(); err != nil {
97			fmt.Fprintln(os.Stderr, "error:", err)
98			os.Exit(1)
99		}
100	}

Claude

I've diagnosed everything. Here's what I found and what I propose.

Findings

--project is effectively broken. It's only consulted inside latestSession(), i.e. it does nothing unless you also pass --latest. Running ccwhid --project foo alone falls through to the default branch in resolveSession (run.go:37) в†’ opens the TUI and ignores --project entirely. That's exactly the "didn't work with name or path" you hit.

The "subagent sessions" are real separate files, not sidechains. Your SDD reviews each ran as SDK-spawned agents that Claude Code wrote as their own top-level transcripts (16 files here; only 1 is yours). They're cleanly distinguishable:

Root (yours) Agent-spawned
entrypoint cli sdk-py
promptSource (absent) sdk

So "root session" = entrypoint not starting with sdk (and promptSource != sdk). That's a reliable filter.

Proposed redesign

TUI navigation (two levels + scrolling):

  1. Opens on a project list only (scrollable viewport, в†‘/в†“, sized to terminal).
  2. enter / в†’ on a project в†’ session list for that project (scrollable).
  3. в†ђ / esc / h returns to the project list.
  4. Session list shows root sessions only by default; a key toggles all-sessions on/off (I'll use a, shown in the help line). Agent-spawned count shown as a hint (e.g. "+14 agent sessions вЂ” press a").
  5. enter on a session в†’ the existing Options screen (subagents/redact/open/generate), unchanged.

Terminal-size-aware viewport via Bubble Tea's WindowSizeMsg, with a scroll window so long lists page properly.

--project fix: improve matching (prefer exact path, then basename, then unambiguous substring) and make it work standalone вЂ” see the question below.

I'll also fold the same root/agent classification into discovery so --latest/--project target your sessions by default rather than a review agent's.

One decision I need from you:

Claude

23		dir := t.TempDir()
24		src := filepath.Join(dir, "sess.jsonl")
25		lines := strings.Join([]string{
26			`{"type":"ai-title","aiTitle":"Test run"}`,
27			`{"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":"hello"},"timestamp":"2026-07-11T10:00:00Z"}`,
28			`{"type":"assistant","message":{"role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"text","text":"world"}]},"timestamp":"2026-07-11T10:00:01Z"}`,
29		}, "\n")
30		if err := os.WriteFile(src, []byte(lines), 0o644); err != nil {
31			t.Fatal(err)
32		}
33		out := filepath.Join(dir, "report")
34		opts := &options{out: out, includeSubagents: true}
35		si := discovery.SessionInfo{ID: "sess", FilePath: src}
36		got, err := generate(opts, si)
37		if err != nil {
38			t.Fatal(err)
39		}
40		if got != out {
41			t.Errorf("generate returned %q, want %q", got, out)
42		}
43		html, err := os.ReadFile(filepath.Join(out, "index.html"))
44		if err != nil {
45			t.Fatal(err)
46		}
47		if !strings.Contains(string(html), "Test run") || !strings.Contains(string(html), "world") {
48			t.Error("report missing expected content")
49		}

1	package discovery

10	
11	func TestEncodeDecodeRoundTrip(t *testing.T) {
12		// NOTE: deviates from the task brief's literal fixture, which used
13		// "~/IdeaProjects/cc-what-have-i-done" (this repo's own
14		// path). That path contains a literal hyphen in the directory name
15		// ("cc-what-have-i-done"), which the naive '/'<->'-' replace scheme
16		// specified below cannot round-trip: every embedded hyphen gets
17		// decoded back into a '/'. This is a mathematical property of the
18		// scheme, not an implementation bug, so a hyphen-free path is used
19		// here instead to exercise a genuinely invertible case. See the
20		// task report for verification (go run of the exact replace calls
21		// against the original fixture).
22		cwd := "~/IdeaProjects/ccwhid"
23		enc := EncodeProjectDir(cwd)
24		if enc != "-Users-markus-IdeaProjects-ccwhid" {
25			t.Fatalf("EncodeProjectDir = %q", enc)
26		}
27		if dec := DecodeProjectDir(enc); dec != cwd {
28			t.Fatalf("DecodeProjectDir = %q, want %q", dec, cwd)
29		}
30	}
31	
32	// writeSession writes a minimal valid jsonl file with the given lines.
33	func writeSession(t *testing.T, dir, id string, lines ...string) {
34		t.Helper()
35		if err := os.MkdirAll(dir, 0o755); err != nil {
36			t.Fatal(err)
37		}
38		path := filepath.Join(dir, id+".jsonl")
39		data := ""
40		for _, l := range lines {
41			data += l + "\n"
42		}
43		if err := os.WriteFile(path, []byte(data), 0o644); err != nil {
44			t.Fatal(err)
45		}
46	}
47	
48	func TestTruncateRuneSafe(t *testing.T) {
49		s := strings.Repeat("Г¤", 80)
50		got := truncate(s, 60)
51		if !utf8.ValidString(got) {
52			t.Errorf("truncate produced invalid UTF-8: %q", got)
53		}
54	}
55

85	}

Edit~/IdeaProjects/cc-what-have-i-done/internal/discovery/discovery.go
- sc := bufio.NewScanner(f)
- sc.Buffer(make([]byte, 0, 1024*1024), 16*1024*1024)
- cwdSet := false
- for sc.Scan() {
- var l scanLine
- if err := json.Unmarshal(sc.Bytes(), &l); err != nil {
- continue // tolerate malformed lines
- }
- switch l.Type {
- case "ai-title":
- if l.AiTitle != "" {
- info.Title = l.AiTitle
- }
- case "user", "assistant":

+ sc.Buffer(make([]byte, 0, 1024*1024), 16*1024*1024)
+ cwdSet := false
+ entrypointSet := false
+ for sc.Scan() {
+ var l scanLine
+ if err := json.Unmarshal(sc.Bytes(), &l); err != nil {
+ continue // tolerate malformed lines
+ }
+ switch l.Type {
+ case "ai-title":
+ if l.AiTitle != "" {
+ info.Title = l.AiTitle
+ }
+ case "user", "assistant":
+ info.MessageCount++
+ if l.IsSidechain {
+ info.HasSubagents = true
+ }
+ // Classify origin: the first record carrying an entrypoint decides
+ // it (interactive "cli"/IDE vs. "sdk-*"), and any prompt sourced
+ // from the SDK confirms an agent-spawned transcript.
+ if !entrypointSet && l.Entrypoint != "" {
+ info.IsAgent = strings.HasPrefix(l.Entrypoint, "sdk")
+ entrypointSet = true
+ }
+ if l.PromptSource == "sdk" {
+ info.IsAgent = true
+ }

Now add FindProject and helper methods to discovery. Let me add after FindSession:

Claude
Edit~/IdeaProjects/cc-what-have-i-done/internal/discovery/discovery.go
- // DisplayLabel returns a human-friendly one-line label for a session.
+ // RootSessions returns the group's interactive (non-agent) sessions, preserving
+ // order.
+ func (g ProjectGroup) RootSessions() []SessionInfo {
+ out := make([]SessionInfo, 0, len(g.Sessions))
+ for _, s := range g.Sessions {
+ if !s.IsAgent {
+ out = append(out, s)
+ }
+ }
+ return out
+ }
+
+ // AgentCount returns how many of the group's sessions were agent-spawned.
+ func (g ProjectGroup) AgentCount() int {
+ n := 0
+ for _, s := range g.Sessions {
+ if s.IsAgent {
+ n++
+ }
+ }
+ return n
+ }
+
+ // FindProject resolves a project selector (full path, basename, or unambiguous
+ // substring of the path) to an index into groups. It errors if nothing matches
+ // or the selector is ambiguous.
+ func FindProject(groups []ProjectGroup, want string) (int, error) {
+ // 1. Exact absolute-path match.
+ for i, g := range groups {
+ if g.ProjectPath == want {
+ return i, nil
+ }
+ }
+ // 2. Case-insensitive basename match.
+ var matches []int
+ for i, g := range groups {
+ if strings.EqualFold(filepath.Base(g.ProjectPath), want) {
+ matches = append(matches, i)
+ }
+ }
+ // 3. Fall back to a case-insensitive substring of the full path.
+ if len(matches) == 0 {
+ lw := strings.ToLower(want)
+ for i, g := range groups {
+ if strings.Contains(strings.ToLower(g.ProjectPath), lw) {
+ matches = append(matches, i)
+ }
+ }
+ }
+ switch len(matches) {
+ case 0:
+ return -1, fmt.Errorf("no project matching %q", want)
+ case 1:
+ return matches[0], nil
+ default:
+ return -1, fmt.Errorf("ambiguous project %q matches %d projects", want, len(matches))
+ }
+ }
+
+ // DisplayLabel returns a human-friendly one-line label for a session.

Now the core rewrite вЂ” tui.go with two-level navigation, a scrolling viewport, and the root/all toggle:

Write~/IdeaProjects/cc-what-have-i-done/internal/tui/tui.go
+ // Package tui provides an interactive session browser used when ccwhid is run
+ // with no selector flags. It presents a two-level view: a scrollable list of
+ // projects, then a scrollable list of that project's sessions.
+ package tui
+
+ import (
+ "fmt"
+ "strings"
+
+ tea "github.com/charmbracelet/bubbletea"
+ "github.com/charmbracelet/lipgloss"
+
+ "github.com/saigyo/cc-what-have-i-done/internal/discovery"
+ )
+
+ // Selection is the result of running the browser.
+ type Selection struct {
+ Session discovery.SessionInfo
+ IncludeSubagents bool
+ Redact bool
+ Open bool
+ OutDir string
+ Canceled bool
+ }
+
+ var (
+ titleStyle = lipgloss.NewStyle().Bold(true)
+ headerStyle = lipgloss.NewStyle().Bold(true).Foreground(lipgloss.Color("#D97757"))
+ selectedStyle = lipgloss.NewStyle().Foreground(lipgloss.Color("#1A1A18")).Background(lipgloss.Color("#F6E7DF"))
+ mutedStyle = lipgloss.NewStyle().Foreground(lipgloss.Color("240"))
+ optionStyle = lipgloss.NewStyle().Foreground(lipgloss.Color("#D97757"))
+ )
+
+ type screen int
+
+ const (
+ screenProjects screen = iota
+ screenSessions
+ screenOptions
+ )
+
+ // reservedLines is how many rows the title and footer occupy, leaving the rest
+ // of the terminal height for the scrollable list body.
+ const reservedLines = 4
+
+ type model struct {
+ groups []discovery.ProjectGroup
+
+ // projects screen
+ projCursor int
+ projTop int
+
+ // sessions screen
+ groupIdx int
+ showAll bool
+ sessions []discovery.SessionInfo // filtered view of groups[groupIdx]
+ sessCursor int
+ sessTop int
+
+ // options screen
+ optCursor int
+
+ screen screen
+ sel Selection
+
+ height int
+ width int
+ }
+
+ func newModel(groups []discovery.ProjectGroup) model {
+ return model{
+ groups: groups,
+ screen: screenProjects,
+ height: 20,
+ width: 80,
+ sel: Selection{
+ IncludeSubagents: true,
+ Redact: true,
+ },
+ }
+ }
+
+ // listHeight is the number of list rows visible in the current terminal.
+ func (m model) listHeight() int {
+ h := m.height - reservedLines
+ if h < 1 {
+ return 1
+ }
+ return h
+ }
+
+ func (m model) Init() tea.Cmd { return nil }
+
+ func (m model) Update(msg tea.Msg) (tea.Model, tea.Cmd) {
+ switch msg := msg.(type) {
+ case tea.WindowSizeMsg:
+ m.height = msg.Height
+ m.width = msg.Width
+ m.adjustProjScroll()
+ m.adjustSessScroll()
+ return m, nil
+ case tea.KeyMsg:
+ switch m.screen {
+ case screenProjects:
+ return m.updateProjects(msg)
+ case screenSessions:
+ return m.updateSessions(msg)
+ default:
+ return m.updateOptions(msg)
+ }
+ }
+ return m, nil
+ }
+
+ // --- projects screen ---
+
+ func (m model) updateProjects(key tea.KeyMsg) (tea.Model, tea.Cmd) {
+ switch key.String() {
+ case "ctrl+c", "q", "esc":
+ m.sel.Canceled = true
+ return m, tea.Quit
+ case "up", "k":
+ if m.projCursor > 0 {
+ m.projCursor--
+ m.adjustProjScroll()
+ }
+ case "down", "j":
+ if m.projCursor < len(m.groups)-1 {
+ m.projCursor++
+ m.adjustProjScroll()
+ }
+ case "enter", "right", "l":
+ if len(m.groups) > 0 {
+ m.enterProject(m.projCursor)
+ }
+ }
+ return m, nil
+ }
+
+ func (m *model) adjustProjScroll() {
+ m.projTop = clampScroll(m.projCursor, m.projTop, m.listHeight(), len(m.groups))
+ }
+
+ func (m *model) enterProject(idx int) {
+ m.groupIdx = idx
+ m.showAll = false
+ m.sessCursor = 0
+ m.sessTop = 0
+ m.refreshSessions()
+ m.screen = screenSessions
+ }
+
+ func (m *model) refreshSessions() {
+ g := m.groups[m.groupIdx]
+ if m.showAll {
+ m.sessions = g.Sessions
+ } else {
+ m.sessions = g.RootSessions()
+ }
+ if m.sessCursor >= len(m.sessions) {
+ m.sessCursor = max(0, len(m.sessions)-1)
+ }
+ m.adjustSessScroll()
+ }
+
+ // --- sessions screen ---
+
+ func (m model) updateSessions(key tea.KeyMsg) (tea.Model, tea.Cmd) {
+ switch key.String() {
+ case "ctrl+c", "q":
+ m.sel.Canceled = true
+ return m, tea.Quit
+ case "esc", "left", "h":
+ m.screen = screenProjects
+ case "up", "k":
+ if m.sessCursor > 0 {
+ m.sessCursor--
+ m.adjustSessScroll()
+ }
+ case "down", "j":
+ if m.sessCursor < len(m.sessions)-1 {
+ m.sessCursor++
+ m.adjustSessScroll()
+ }
+ case "a":
+ m.showAll = !m.showAll
+ m.sessCursor = 0
+ m.sessTop = 0
+ m.refreshSessions()
+ case "enter", "right", "l":
+ if len(m.sessions) > 0 {
+ m.sel.Session = m.sessions[m.sessCursor]
+ m.optCursor = 0
+ m.screen = screenOptions
+ }
+ }
+ return m, nil
+ }
+
+ func (m *model) adjustSessScroll() {
+ m.sessTop = clampScroll(m.sessCursor, m.sessTop, m.listHeight(), len(m.sessions))
+ }
+
+ // --- options screen ---
+
+ // optionCount is the number of toggle rows plus the Generate action.
+ const optionCount = 4 // subagents, redact, open, generate
+
+ func (m model) updateOptions(key tea.KeyMsg) (tea.Model, tea.Cmd) {
+ switch key.String() {
+ case "ctrl+c", "q":
+ m.sel.Canceled = true
+ return m, tea.Quit
+ case "esc", "left", "h":
+ m.screen = screenSessions
+ case "up", "k":
+ if m.optCursor > 0 {
+ m.optCursor--
+ }
+ case "down", "j":
+ if m.optCursor < optionCount-1 {
+ m.optCursor++
+ }
+ case " ", "enter":
+ switch m.optCursor {
+ case 0:
+ m.sel.IncludeSubagents = !m.sel.IncludeSubagents
+ case 1:
+ m.sel.Redact = !m.sel.Redact
+ case 2:
+ m.sel.Open = !m.sel.Open
+ case 3:
+ return m, tea.Quit
+ }
+ }
+ return m, nil
+ }
+
+ // clampScroll returns a scroll offset that keeps cursor within the visible
+ // window [top, top+visible) over a list of length n.
+ func clampScroll(cursor, top, visible, n int) int {
+ if visible < 1 {
+ visible = 1
+ }
+ if cursor < top {
+ top = cursor
+ }
+ if cursor >= top+visible {
+ top = cursor - visible + 1
+ }
+ if top < 0 {
+ top = 0
+ }
+ // Don't scroll past the end when the list shrank.
+ if max := n - visible; top > max && max >= 0 {
+ top = max
+ }
+ return top
+ }
+
+ func (m model) View() string {
+ switch m.screen {
+ case screenProjects:
+ return m.viewProjects()
+ case screenSessions:
+ return m.viewSessions()
+ default:
+ return m.viewOptions()
+ }
+ }
+
+ func (m model) viewProjects() string {
+ var b strings.Builder
+ b.WriteString(titleStyle.Render("Select a project") +
+ mutedStyle.Render(" в†‘/в†“ move В· enter open В· q quit") + "\n\n")
+ visible := m.listHeight()
+ end := min(m.projTop+visible, len(m.groups))
+ for i := m.projTop; i < end; i++ {
+ g := m.groups[i]
+ roots := len(g.RootSessions())
+ agents := g.AgentCount()
+ count := fmt.Sprintf("%d session%s", roots, plural(roots))
+ if agents > 0 {
+ count += fmt.Sprintf(", %d agent", agents)
+ }
+ label := headerStyle.Render(g.ProjectPath) + " " + mutedStyle.Render(count)
+ if i == m.projCursor {
+ label = selectedStyle.Render("в–ё " + g.ProjectPath + " " + count)
+ } else {
+ label = " " + label
+ }
+ b.WriteString(label + "\n")
+ }
+ b.WriteString(scrollHint(m.projTop, end, len(m.groups)))
+ return b.String()
+ }
+
+ func (m model) viewSessions() string {
+ var b strings.Builder
+ g := m.groups[m.groupIdx]
+ b.WriteString(titleStyle.Render("Sessions in ") + headerStyle.Render(g.ProjectPath) + "\n")
+ toggle := "a show all"
+ if m.showAll {
+ toggle = "a root only"
+ }
+ b.WriteString(mutedStyle.Render("в†‘/в†“ move В· enter select В· в†ђ back В· "+toggle+" В· q quit") + "\n\n")
+
+ if len(m.sessions) == 0 {
+ b.WriteString(mutedStyle.Render(" no interactive sessions here вЂ” press a to show agent sessions") + "\n")
+ return b.String()
+ }
+ visible := m.listHeight()
+ end := min(m.sessTop+visible, len(m.sessions))
+ for i := m.sessTop; i < end; i++ {
+ s := m.sessions[i]
+ id := s.ID[:min(8, len(s.ID))]
+ tag := ""
+ if s.IsAgent {
+ tag = mutedStyle.Render(" вџІ")
+ }
+ line := fmt.Sprintf(" %s %s%s", s.DisplayLabel(), mutedStyle.Render(id), tag)
+ if i == m.sessCursor {
+ line = selectedStyle.Render("в–ё "+s.DisplayLabel()+" "+id) + tag
+ }
+ b.WriteString(line + "\n")
+ }
+ b.WriteString(scrollHint(m.sessTop, end, len(m.sessions)))
+ return b.String()
+ }
+
+ func (m model) viewOptions() string {
+ var b strings.Builder
+ b.WriteString("Options for: " + m.sel.Session.DisplayLabel() + "\n\n")
+ toggles := []struct {
+ label string
+ on bool
+ }{
+ {"Include subagents", m.sel.IncludeSubagents},
+ {"Redact secrets", m.sel.Redact},
+ {"Open in browser when done", m.sel.Open},
+ }
+ for i, t := range toggles {
+ check := "[ ]"
+ if t.on {
+ check = "[x]"
+ }
+ line := fmt.Sprintf("%s %s", check, t.label)
+ if m.optCursor == i {
+ line = optionStyle.Render("в–ё " + line)
+ } else {
+ line = " " + line
+ }
+ b.WriteString(line + "\n")
+ }
+ gen := "Generate report"
+ if m.optCursor == 3 {
+ gen = optionStyle.Render("в–ё " + gen)
+ } else {
+ gen = " " + gen
+ }
+ b.WriteString("\n" + gen + "\n\n")
+ b.WriteString(mutedStyle.Render("space toggle В· enter confirm В· esc back В· q quit") + "\n")
+ return b.String()
+ }
+
+ // scrollHint renders a one-line position indicator when the list is scrolled or
+ // overflows the viewport.
+ func scrollHint(top, end, n int) string {
+ if top == 0 && end >= n {
+ return ""
+ }
+ return mutedStyle.Render(fmt.Sprintf("\n %dвЂ“%d of %d", top+1, end, n))
+ }
+
+ func plural(n int) string {
+ if n == 1 {
+ return ""
+ }
+ return "s"
+ }
+
+ // Run launches the browser and returns the user's selection. If focusIdx is a
+ // valid index into groups, the browser opens directly on that project's session
+ // list; pass -1 to start on the project list.
+ func Run(groups []discovery.ProjectGroup, focusIdx int) (Selection, error) {
+ if len(groups) == 0 {
+ return Selection{Canceled: true}, fmt.Errorf("no sessions found under ~/.claude/projects")
+ }
+ m := newModel(groups)
+ if focusIdx >= 0 && focusIdx < len(groups) {
+ m.projCursor = focusIdx
+ m.enterProject(focusIdx)
+ }
+ p := tea.NewProgram(m, tea.WithAltScreen())
+ res, err := p.Run()
+ if err != nil {
+ return Selection{}, err
+ }
+ fm := res.(model)
+ return fm.sel, nil
+ }
+

+ // latestSession returns the most recent interactive (non-agent) session,
+ // optionally scoped to a project. Agent-spawned transcripts are skipped so
+ // --latest targets the user's own sessions.
+ func latestSession(opts *options, root string) (discovery.SessionInfo, bool, error) {
+ groups, err := discovery.Scan(root)
+ if err != nil {
+ return discovery.SessionInfo{}, false, err
+ }
+ if opts.project != "" {
+ idx, err := discovery.FindProject(groups, opts.project)
+ if err != nil {
+ return discovery.SessionInfo{}, false, err
+ }
+ groups = groups[idx : idx+1]
+ }
+ for _, g := range groups {
+ for _, s := range g.Sessions {
+ if !s.IsAgent {
+ return s, false, nil
+ }
+ }
+ }
+ return discovery.SessionInfo{}, false, fmt.Errorf("no sessions found")
+ }

Write~/IdeaProjects/cc-what-have-i-done/internal/tui/tui_test.go
+ package tui
+
+ import (
+ "testing"
+
+ tea "github.com/charmbracelet/bubbletea"
+
+ "github.com/saigyo/cc-what-have-i-done/internal/discovery"
+ )
+
+ func testGroups() []discovery.ProjectGroup {
+ return []discovery.ProjectGroup{
+ {
+ ProjectPath: "/tmp/projA",
+ Sessions: []discovery.SessionInfo{
+ {ID: "root1aaa-0000", Title: "Root one"},
+ {ID: "agent1aa-0000", Title: "Agent one", IsAgent: true},
+ {ID: "root2aaa-0000", Title: "Root two"},
+ },
+ },
+ {
+ ProjectPath: "/tmp/projB",
+ Sessions: []discovery.SessionInfo{{ID: "root3bbb-0000", Title: "Root three"}},
+ },
+ }
+ }
+
+ func key(s string) tea.KeyMsg {
+ switch s {
+ case "enter":
+ return tea.KeyMsg{Type: tea.KeyEnter}
+ case "left":
+ return tea.KeyMsg{Type: tea.KeyLeft}
+ case "down":
+ return tea.KeyMsg{Type: tea.KeyDown}
+ case "up":
+ return tea.KeyMsg{Type: tea.KeyUp}
+ default:
+ return tea.KeyMsg{Type: tea.KeyRunes, Runes: []rune(s)}
+ }
+ }
+
+ func send(m model, msgs ...tea.Msg) model {
+ var tm tea.Model = m
+ for _, msg := range msgs {
+ tm, _ = tm.Update(msg)
+ }
+ return tm.(model)
+ }
+
+ func TestSessionListHidesAgentsByDefault(t *testing.T) {
+ m := newModel(testGroups())
+ m = send(m, key("enter")) // open projA
+ if m.screen != screenSessions {
+ t.Fatalf("screen = %v, want sessions", m.screen)
+ }
+ if len(m.sessions) != 2 {
+ t.Fatalf("root sessions = %d, want 2 (agents hidden)", len(m.sessions))
+ }
+ for _, s := range m.sessions {
+ if s.IsAgent {
+ t.Errorf("agent session %q leaked into default list", s.ID)
+ }
+ }
+ }
+
+ func TestToggleShowAllRevealsAgents(t *testing.T) {
+ m := newModel(testGroups())
+ m = send(m, key("enter"), key("a"))
+ if !m.showAll {
+ t.Fatal("showAll not toggled")
+ }
+ if len(m.sessions) != 3 {
+ t.Fatalf("all sessions = %d, want 3", len(m.sessions))
+ }
+ m = send(m, key("a"))
+ if m.showAll || len(m.sessions) != 2 {
+ t.Fatalf("toggle back failed: showAll=%v n=%d", m.showAll, len(m.sessions))
+ }
+ }
+
+ func TestLeftReturnsToProjectList(t *testing.T) {
+ m := newModel(testGroups())
+ m = send(m, key("enter"))
+ if m.screen != screenSessions {
+ t.Fatalf("screen = %v, want sessions", m.screen)
+ }
+ m = send(m, key("left"))
+ if m.screen != screenProjects {
+ t.Fatalf("screen = %v, want projects after left", m.screen)
+ }
+ }
+
+ func TestSelectSessionGoesToOptions(t *testing.T) {
+ m := newModel(testGroups())
+ m = send(m, key("enter"), key("enter")) // open projA, select first session
+ if m.screen != screenOptions {
+ t.Fatalf("screen = %v, want options", m.screen)
+ }
+ if m.sel.Session.ID != "root1aaa-0000" {
+ t.Errorf("selected %q, want root1aaa-0000", m.sel.Session.ID)
+ }
+ }
+
+ func TestScrollKeepsCursorVisible(t *testing.T) {
+ // 30 sessions, viewport of 10 rows.
+ var ss []discovery.SessionInfo
+ for i := 0; i < 30; i++ {
+ ss = append(ss, discovery.SessionInfo{ID: string(rune('a'+i%26)) + "0000000", Title: "s"})
+ }
+ m := newModel([]discovery.ProjectGroup{{ProjectPath: "/p", Sessions: ss}})
+ m = send(m, tea.WindowSizeMsg{Width: 80, Height: reservedLines + 10}, key("enter"))
+ for i := 0; i < 25; i++ {
+ m = send(m, key("down"))
+ }
+ if m.sessCursor != 25 {
+ t.Fatalf("cursor = %d, want 25", m.sessCursor)
+ }
+ // cursor must be within the visible window [top, top+10)
+ if m.sessCursor < m.sessTop || m.sessCursor >= m.sessTop+m.listHeight() {
+ t.Errorf("cursor %d outside window [%d,%d)", m.sessCursor, m.sessTop, m.sessTop+m.listHeight())
+ }
+ }
+
+ func TestFocusIdxOpensSessionList(t *testing.T) {
+ m := newModel(testGroups())
+ m.projCursor = 1
+ m.enterProject(1)
+ if m.screen != screenSessions {
+ t.Fatalf("screen = %v, want sessions", m.screen)
+ }
+ if m.sessions[0].ID != "root3bbb-0000" {
+ t.Errorf("focused group session = %q, want root3bbb-0000", m.sessions[0].ID)
+ }
+ }
+
+ func TestClampScroll(t *testing.T) {
+ // cursor below window scrolls down
+ if got := clampScroll(12, 0, 10, 30); got != 3 {
+ t.Errorf("clampScroll down = %d, want 3", got)
+ }
+ // cursor above window scrolls up
+ if got := clampScroll(2, 5, 10, 30); got != 2 {
+ t.Errorf("clampScroll up = %d, want 2", got)
+ }
+ // list shorter than window pins to 0
+ if got := clampScroll(0, 4, 10, 3); got != 0 {
+ t.Errorf("clampScroll short = %d, want 0", got)
+ }
+ }
+

+ func TestFindProject(t *testing.T) {
+ groups := []ProjectGroup{
+ {ProjectPath: "/Users/x/IdeaProjects/cc-what-have-i-done"},
+ {ProjectPath: "/Users/x/IdeaProjects/other-app"},
+ {ProjectPath: "/Users/x/Downloads/apparatus"},

+ want string
+ wantIdx int
+ wantErr bool
+ }{
+ {"/Users/x/IdeaProjects/other-app", 1, false}, // exact path
+ {"cc-what-have-i-done", 0, false}, // basename
+ {"OTHER-APP", 1, false}, // basename, case-insensitive
+ {"Downloads", 2, false}, // substring
+ {"nope", -1, true}, // no match
+ {"IdeaProjects", -1, true}, // ambiguous substring
+ }
+ for _, c := range cases {
+ idx, err := FindProject(groups, c.want)
+ if c.wantErr {
+ if err == nil {
+ t.Errorf("FindProject(%q) = %d, want error", c.want, idx)
+ }
+ continue
+ }
+ if err != nil || idx != c.wantIdx {
+ t.Errorf("FindProject(%q) = %d, %v; want %d", c.want, idx, err, c.wantIdx)
+ }
+ }
+ }

All tests pass, build and vet are clean. I verified the classification, scroll math, FindProject, and TUI empty-state paths against the actual code. Here is the review.

## Findings

### Important вЂ” `latestSession` does not return the globally newest interactive session
File: `cmd/ccwhid/run.go:54-63` (the skip loop in `latestSession`)

Spec item 4 says `--latest` should "target the newest interactive session (in or out of a project scope)." The implementation instead returns the first non-agent session in **group order**, and groups are ordered by each group's *newest session including agents* (`Scan` sorts by `groups[i].Sessions[0].ModTime`, and `Sessions[0]` may be an agent transcript). So it finds "the newest interactive session inside whichever project had the most recent activity of any kind," not the newest interactive session overall.

Failure scenario (no `--project`):
- Project A sessions: `agent@T=100`, `interactive@T=50`
- Project B sessions: `interactive@T=90`

`Scan` orders A before B (100 > 90). The loop enters A, skips the agent, and returns `interactive@T=50`. But the newest interactive session is B's `@T=90`. `--latest` renders the wrong (older) session. This is very plausible in practice: running a code-review/Task agent in project A writes a fresh top-level transcript with a recent mtime, while your actual latest human session was in project B.

Note the old code (`return groups[0].Sessions[0]`) was correct for "newest session" because the group sort key *is* `Sessions[0].ModTime`; adding the agent-skip broke that invariant without switching to a global max.

Suggested fix: scan all sessions and pick the non-agent one with the maximum `ModTime`, e.g.
```go
var best *discovery.SessionInfo
for _, g := range groups {
    for i := range g.Sessions {
        s := g.Sessions[i]
        if s.IsAgent {
            continue
        }
        if best == nil || s.ModTime.After(best.ModTime) {
            best = &s
        }
    }
}
if best == nil { return ..., fmt.Errorf("no sessions found") }
return *best, false, nil
```
(The `--project` scoped path narrows to one group first, where this reduces to the correct newest-interactive-in-group.)

## Verified correct (no defect)

- **`clampScroll`** вЂ” Boundary math is correct. For `n=0`/empty lists it returns 0 (the `max := n - visible; max >= 0` guard is skipped, and the cursor-pull clauses keep `top=0`). I checked the potential "stale large `top` when `visible > n`" stranding case: `sessTop`/`sessCursor` are reset to 0 on both `enterProject` and the `a` toggle (the only places `n` changes), and `WindowSizeMsg` changes only `visible`, never `n`, so a stale oversized `top` is unreachable. The `max >= 0` guard is effectively dead but harmless.
- **WindowSizeMsg / defaults** вЂ” `height` defaults to 20; `listHeight()` clamps to `>= 1`; keys before the first size msg are safe.
- **Empty states** вЂ” `enter`/`right` in both screens is guarded by `len(...) > 0`; `viewSessions` early-returns the "press a" hint on empty; `refreshSessions` clamps `sessCursor` via `max(0, len-1)`. No slicing panics. A `--project` match with zero root sessions opens a non-crashing empty session list. All confirmed.
- **Agent classification** (`discovery.go:120-129`) вЂ” Matches the spec: first entrypoint-bearing user/assistant record decides via `HasPrefix("sdk")` and latches with `entrypointSet`; `promptSource=="sdk"` can only set `IsAgent=true` (never resets), so an sdk session can't be un-classified by a later non-sdk record, and a cli session flips to agent only if a record actually carries `promptSource=="sdk"`. Entrypoint-absent + `promptSource=="sdk"` correctly yields agent. A file with no user/assistant records stays `IsAgent=false` (shown by default) вЂ” acceptable per spec.
- **`FindProject`** вЂ” Exact path precedence, then case-insensitive basename, then case-insensitive substring; ambiguity/no-match errors are correct. `groups[idx:idx+1]` is bounds-safe.

## Minor

- **Test gap for the Important bug:** `latestSession` in `run.go` has no test at all вЂ” neither the agent-skip nor the ordering. A cheap table test over synthetic groups (like the counterexample above) would have caught the ordering defect. The new discovery/tui tests are meaningful and non-vacuous, but this untested seam is exactly where the bug lives.
- **Entrypoint only read on `user`/`assistant` records** (`discovery.go:110-137`): if a real transcript carries `entrypoint` only on some other record type (e.g. a summary/system line), classification would miss it. The author's test assumes entrypoint-on-user, so this is a schema-assumption risk rather than a confirmed bug вЂ” worth a comment or a quick check against a real agent transcript.

No other issues above Minor.
agentId: ad1bfe0b3beb4138b (use SendMessage with to: 'ad1bfe0b3beb4138b', summary: '<5-10 word recap>' to continue this agent)
<usage>subagent_tokens: 59996
tool_uses: 7
duration_ms: 139767</usage>
Claude

The reviewer found one Important bug: --latest returns the first interactive session in group order, but groups are ordered by their newest session including agents вЂ” so --latest can render an older interactive session instead of the globally newest one. Concrete failure: an agent run in project A bumps A ahead of project B, and --latest returns A's older human session instead of B's newer one. That's a real regression from my agent-skip change. Let me fix it and close the test gap.

Claude

+ if opts.project != "" {
+ idx, err := discovery.FindProject(groups, opts.project)
+ if err != nil {
+ return discovery.SessionInfo{}, false, err
+ }
+ groups = groups[idx : idx+1]
+ }
+ // Pick the newest interactive session by modification time. Group order
+ // alone is insufficient: groups are sorted by their newest session
+ // *including* agent transcripts, so a recent agent run in one project
+ // could otherwise mask a newer human session in another.
+ bestGI, bestSI := -1, -1
+ for gi := range groups {
+ for si := range groups[gi].Sessions {
+ if groups[gi].Sessions[si].IsAgent {
+ continue
+ }
+ if bestGI < 0 || groups[gi].Sessions[si].ModTime.After(groups[bestGI].Sessions[bestSI].ModTime) {
+ bestGI, bestSI = gi, si
+ }
+ }
+ }
+ if bestGI < 0 {
+ return discovery.SessionInfo{}, false, fmt.Errorf("no sessions found")
+ }
+ return groups[bestGI].Sessions[bestSI], false, nil

Edit~/IdeaProjects/cc-what-have-i-done/cmd/ccwhid/run_test.go
- import (
- "os"
- "path/filepath"
- "strings"
- "testing"
-
- "github.com/saigyo/cc-what-have-i-done/internal/discovery"
- )
+ import (
+ "fmt"
+ "os"
+ "path/filepath"
+ "strings"
+ "testing"
+ "time"
+
+ "github.com/saigyo/cc-what-have-i-done/internal/discovery"
+ )
+
+ // writeLatestSession writes a one-line transcript with a controlled mtime so
+ // latestSession's newest-first selection can be exercised deterministically.
+ func writeLatestSession(t *testing.T, root, projDir, id, entrypoint, promptSource string, mod time.Time) {
+ t.Helper()
+ dir := filepath.Join(root, projDir)
+ if err := os.MkdirAll(dir, 0o755); err != nil {
+ t.Fatal(err)
+ }
+ p := filepath.Join(dir, id+".jsonl")
+ line := fmt.Sprintf(`{"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":"x"},"entrypoint":%q,"promptSource":%q,"cwd":%q,"timestamp":"2026-07-11T10:00:00Z"}`,
+ entrypoint, promptSource, "/"+projDir)
+ if err := os.WriteFile(p, []byte(line+"\n"), 0o644); err != nil {
+ t.Fatal(err)
+ }
+ if err := os.Chtimes(p, mod, mod); err != nil {
+ t.Fatal(err)
+ }
+ }
+
+ func TestLatestSessionPicksNewestInteractive(t *testing.T) {
+ root := t.TempDir()
+ base := time.Date(2026, 7, 11, 10, 0, 0, 0, time.UTC)
+ // Project A: newest file is an agent transcript; its interactive one is older.
+ writeLatestSession(t, root, "-a", "aaaaaaaa-0000-0000-0000-000000000000", "sdk-py", "sdk", base.Add(100*time.Minute))
+ writeLatestSession(t, root, "-a", "aaaaaaaa-1111-0000-0000-000000000000", "cli", "", base.Add(50*time.Minute))
+ // Project B: interactive, newer than A's interactive but older than A's agent.
+ writeLatestSession(t, root, "-b", "bbbbbbbb-0000-0000-0000-000000000000", "cli", "", base.Add(90*time.Minute))
+
+ // Unscoped: must pick the globally newest interactive session (B), not A's
+ // older interactive session, and never the agent transcript.
+ si, needTUI, err := latestSession(&options{latest: true}, root)
+ if err != nil || needTUI {
+ t.Fatalf("latestSession err=%v needTUI=%v", err, needTUI)
+ }
+ if si.IsAgent {
+ t.Fatal("latestSession returned an agent transcript")
+ }
+ if !strings.HasPrefix(si.ID, "bbbbbbbb") {
+ t.Errorf("unscoped --latest picked %q, want newest interactive bbbbbbbb...", si.ID)
+ }
+
+ // Scoped to project A: must skip the newer agent and return A's interactive.
+ si, _, err = latestSession(&options{latest: true, project: "-a"}, root)
+ if err != nil {
+ t.Fatal(err)
+ }
+ if !strings.HasPrefix(si.ID, "aaaaaaaa-1111") {
+ t.Errorf("--project -a --latest picked %q, want aaaaaaaa-1111...", si.ID)
+ }
+ }
+
+ func TestLatestSessionNoInteractiveErrors(t *testing.T) {
+ root := t.TempDir()
+ base := time.Date(2026, 7, 11, 10, 0, 0, 0, time.UTC)
+ writeLatestSession(t, root, "-a", "aaaaaaaa-0000-0000-0000-000000000000", "sdk-py", "sdk", base)
+ if _, _, err := latestSession(&options{latest: true, project: "-a"}, root); err == nil {
+ t.Error("expected error when project has only agent sessions")
+ }
+ }

Claude
Read~/IdeaProjects/cc-what-have-i-done/README.md
{
  "file_path": "~/IdeaProjects/cc-what-have-i-done/README.md"
}
1	# ccwhid вЂ” cc-what-have-i-done
2	
3	Turn a Claude Code session transcript into a browsable, self-contained static
4	HTML report. See what you prompted and what Claude Code did вЂ” and commit the
5	report into your repo as a documentation artifact.
6	
7	> **Status:** under active development. See
8	> [`docs/superpowers/plans/`](docs/superpowers/plans/) for the implementation plan.
9	
10	## Install
11	
12	```bash
13	go install github.com/saigyo/cc-what-have-i-done/cmd/ccwhid@latest
14	```
15	
16	Or build locally:
17	
18	```bash
19	go build -o ccwhid ./cmd/ccwhid
20	```
21	
22	## Usage
23	
24	```bash
25	ccwhid                      # browse sessions in an interactive TUI
26	ccwhid --latest             # render the most recent session
27	ccwhid --session <id>       # render a specific session (id or prefix)
28	ccwhid --session <id> --open
29	```
30	
31	The report is written to `./ccwhid-report/<session-short>/` by default (override
32	with `--out`). Open `index.html` in any browser вЂ” no server needed.
33	
34	### Browsing sessions
35	
36	Run `ccwhid` with no selector to open the interactive browser:
37	
38	- **Project list** вЂ” every project with sessions, most-recent first. `в†‘`/`в†“`
39	  to move, `enter` (or `в†’`) to open a project, `q` to quit.
40	- **Session list** вЂ” the chosen project's sessions. `enter` selects, `в†ђ` (or
41	  `esc`) returns to the project list.
42	- Both lists **scroll** to fit any terminal size.
43	- By default only your **interactive sessions** are shown. Claude Code writes
44	  each Task subagent / code-review agent as its own transcript; press **`a`**
45	  in the session list to show (and hide) those agent sessions вЂ” they're marked
46	  with a `вџІ`.
47	
48	`--project <name>` opens the browser directly on that project's session list.
49	
50	### Flags
51	
52	| Flag | Description |
53	|------|-------------|
54	| `--session <id>` | Session id or unambiguous prefix to render |
55	| `--project <path\|name>` | Scope `--latest` to a project, or open the TUI on it (matches full path, basename, or unambiguous substring) |
56	| `--latest` | Render the most recent interactive session (skips agent transcripts) |
57	| `--out <dir>` | Output directory |
58	| `--title <str>` | Override the report title |
59	| `--include-subagents` | Include subagent (Task) activity (default true; `--include-subagents=false` to omit) |
60	| `--no-redact` | Disable secret redaction |
61	| `--force` | Overwrite a non-empty output directory |
62	| `--open` | Open the report in a browser when done |
63	
64	## Redaction
65	
66	By default, ccwhid scrubs common secret shapes (AWS keys, API tokens, JWTs,
67	`KEY=[REDACTED:assignment] assignments) and rewrites your home directory to `~`.
68	This is best-effort defense-in-depth вЂ” **review generated reports before
69	committing them.** Disable with `--no-redact`.
70	
71	## What's included
72	
73	Your prompts, Claude's replies (rendered markdown + syntax-highlighted code),
74	tool calls with collapsible detail, `Edit`/`Write` diffs, collapsed thinking
75	blocks, and вЂ” optionally вЂ” nested subagent activity. System reminders and
76	attachments are omitted for readability.
77	
78	## License
79	
80	[MIT](LICENSE) В© 2026 Markus Ackermann

18	// Options configures a render.
19	type Options struct {
20		Title string
21	}
22	
23	// Site renders the session into outDir as index.html + assets/.
24	func Site(s model.Session, outDir string, opts Options) error {
25		title := opts.Title
26		if title == "" {
27			title = s.DisplayTitle()
28		}
29	
30		tmplSrc, err := assets.ReadFile("assets/report.html.tmpl")
31		if err != nil {
32			return err
33		}
34		tmpl, err := template.New("report").Parse(string(tmplSrc))
35		if err != nil {
36			return err
37		}
38	
39		data := buildViewModel(s, title)
40		var buf bytes.Buffer
41		if err := tmpl.Execute(&buf, data); err != nil {
42			return err
43		}
44	
45		if err := os.MkdirAll(filepath.Join(outDir, "assets"), 0o755); err != nil {
46			return err
47		}
48		if err := os.WriteFile(filepath.Join(outDir, "index.html"), buf.Bytes(), 0o644); err != nil {
49			return err
50		}
51		for _, name := range []string{"styles.css", "app.js"} {
52			b, err := assets.ReadFile("assets/" + name)
53			if err != nil {
54				return err
55			}
56			if err := os.WriteFile(filepath.Join(outDir, "assets", name), b, 0o644); err != nil {
57				return err
58			}
59		}
60		return nil
61	}

63	// view models -------------------------------------------------------------
64	
65	type viewData struct {
66		Title     string
67		Session   model.Session
68		StartedAt string
69		TurnCount int
70		Prompts   []promptRef
71		Turns     []turnView
72	}
73	
74	type promptRef struct {
75		Index   int
76		Preview string
77	}
78	
79	type turnView struct {
80		Index      int
81		Kind       string
82		RoleLabel  string
83		SearchText string
84		Body       template.HTML
85	}
86	
87	func buildViewModel(s model.Session, title string) viewData {
88		d := viewData{
89			Title:     title,
90			Session:   s,
91			TurnCount: len(s.Turns),
92		}
93		if !s.StartedAt.IsZero() {
94			d.StartedAt = s.StartedAt.Format("2006-01-02 15:04")
95		}
96		for i, t := range s.Turns {
97			if t.Kind == model.TurnUser {
98				d.Prompts = append(d.Prompts, promptRef{Index: i, Preview: preview(turnPlainText(t), 60)})
99			}
100			d.Turns = append(d.Turns, turnView{
101				Index:      i,
102				Kind:       string(t.Kind),
103				RoleLabel:  roleLabel(t.Kind),
104				SearchText: strings.ToLower(turnPlainText(t)),
105				Body:       renderTurnBody(t),
106			})
107		}
108		return d
109	}
110	
111	func roleLabel(k model.TurnKind) string {
112		if k == model.TurnUser {
113			return "You"
114		}
115		return "Claude"
116	}
117	
118	// renderTurnBody renders all blocks of a turn to HTML.
119	func renderTurnBody(t model.Turn) template.HTML {
120		var b strings.Builder
121		for _, blk := range t.Blocks {
122			switch blk.Type {
123			case model.BlockText:
124				b.WriteString(string(Markdown(blk.Text)))
125			case model.BlockThinking:
126				b.WriteString(`<details class="thinking"><summary>thinking</summary>`)
127				b.WriteString(string(Markdown(blk.Text)))
128				b.WriteString(`</details>`)
129			case model.BlockToolUse:
130				b.WriteString(renderTool(blk.Tool))
131			}
132		}
133		return template.HTML(b.String())
134	}
135	
136	func renderTool(tc *model.ToolCall) string {
137		var b strings.Builder
138		b.WriteString(`<details class="tool"><summary class="tool-head">`)
139		b.WriteString(`<span class="tool-name">` + html.EscapeString(tc.Name) + `</span>`)
140		if tc.Summary != "" {
141			b.WriteString(`<span class="tool-summary">` + html.EscapeString(tc.Summary) + `</span>`)
142		}
143		b.WriteString(`</summary><div class="tool-body">`)
144		if tc.Diff != nil {
145			b.WriteString(string(DiffHTML(tc.Diff)))
146		} else if tc.InputJSON != "" {
147			b.WriteString(`<pre class="tool-input">` + html.EscapeString(tc.InputJSON) + `</pre>`)
148		}
149		if tc.Result != nil && tc.Result.Content != "" {
150			cls := "tool-result"
151			if tc.Result.IsError {
152				cls += " tool-result-error"
153			}
154			b.WriteString(`<pre class="` + cls + `">` + html.EscapeString(tc.Result.Content) + `</pre>`)
155		}
156		for _, sub := range tc.Subagents {
157			b.WriteString(`<details class="subagent"><summary>subagent: ` + html.EscapeString(sub.Description) + `</summary>`)
158			for _, st := range sub.Turns {
159				b.WriteString(`<article class="turn turn-` + string(st.Kind) + `"><div class="turn-role">` + roleLabel(st.Kind) + `</div><div class="turn-body">`)
160				b.WriteString(string(renderTurnBody(st)))
161				b.WriteString(`</div></article>`)
162			}
163			b.WriteString(`</details>`)
164		}
165		b.WriteString(`</div></details>`)
166		return b.String()
167	}
168	
169	func turnPlainText(t model.Turn) string {
170		var parts []string
171		for _, blk := range t.Blocks {
172			switch blk.Type {
173			case model.BlockText, model.BlockThinking:
174				parts = append(parts, blk.Text)
175			case model.BlockToolUse:
176				parts = append(parts, blk.Tool.Name, blk.Tool.Summary)
177			}
178		}
179		return strings.Join(parts, " ")
180	}
181	
182	func preview(s string, n int) string {
183		s = strings.TrimSpace(strings.ReplaceAll(s, "\n", " "))
184		r := []rune(s)
185		if len(r) <= n {
186			return s
187		}
188		return string(r[:n-1]) + "вЂ¦"
189	}

1	package render
2	
3	import (
4		"bytes"
5		"html"
6		"html/template"
7		"strings"
8	
9		chromahtml "github.com/alecthomas/chroma/v2/formatters/html"
10		"github.com/yuin/goldmark"
11		highlighting "github.com/yuin/goldmark-highlighting/v2"
12		"github.com/yuin/goldmark/extension"
13	
14		"github.com/saigyo/cc-what-have-i-done/internal/model"
15	)
16	
17	// md renders markdown with GFM plus chroma-based syntax highlighting for fenced
18	// code blocks. Highlighting uses inline styles (WithClasses(false)) so the
19	// generated report stays fully self-contained вЂ” no external stylesheet.
20	var md = goldmark.New(goldmark.WithExtensions(
21		extension.GFM,
22		highlighting.NewHighlighting(
23			highlighting.WithStyle("github"),
24			highlighting.WithFormatOptions(
25				chromahtml.WithClasses(false),
26			),
27		),
28	))
29	
30	// Markdown renders CommonMark+GFM to HTML. goldmark runs with its default
31	// Unsafe=false setting, so any raw HTML embedded in the transcript text is
32	// stripped (replaced with an HTML comment) rather than passed through вЂ” the
33	// rendered Body is therefore safe to emit as template.HTML.
34	func Markdown(src string) template.HTML {
35		var buf bytes.Buffer
36		if err := md.Convert([]byte(src), &buf); err != nil {
37			return template.HTML("<pre>" + html.EscapeString(src) + "</pre>")
38		}
39		return template.HTML(buf.String())
40	}
41	
42	// DiffHTML renders a simple line-based diff of a Diff's old/new text.
43	func DiffHTML(d *model.Diff) template.HTML {
44		var b strings.Builder
45		b.WriteString(`<div class="diff">`)
46		if d.OldText != "" {
47			for _, line := range strings.Split(d.OldText, "\n") {
48				b.WriteString(`<div class="diff-del">- `)
49				b.WriteString(html.EscapeString(line))
50				b.WriteString("</div>")
51			}
52		}
53		if d.NewText != "" {
54			for _, line := range strings.Split(d.NewText, "\n") {
55				b.WriteString(`<div class="diff-add">+ `)
56				b.WriteString(html.EscapeString(line))
57				b.WriteString("</div>")
58			}
59		}
60		b.WriteString("</div>")
61		return template.HTML(b.String())
62	}

ANSI codes can appear in several rendered text paths (markdown text blocks, tool results, tool summaries, diffs). I'll add a single StripANSI helper and apply it at each render boundary. First the helper + test:

Claude
Write~/IdeaProjects/cc-what-have-i-done/internal/render/ansi.go
+ package render
+
+ import (
+ "regexp"
+ "strings"
+ )
+
+ // ansiEscape matches ANSI/VT escape sequences: CSI (e.g. SGR colour codes like
+ // "\x1b[1m"), OSC sequences terminated by BEL or ST, and two-character Fe
+ // escapes. Terminal output leaks these into transcripts (e.g. a colourised
+ // `/model` command echo); the ESC byte is invisible in a browser but the
+ // trailing "[1m" shows as literal text, so we strip the whole sequence.
+ var ansiEscape = regexp.MustCompile(`\x1b(?:[@-Z\\-_]|\[[0-?]*[ -/]*[@-~]|\][^\x07\x1b]*(?:\x07|\x1b\\))`)
+
+ // StripANSI removes ANSI escape sequences from s. It fast-paths the common case
+ // of text containing no ESC byte at all.
+ func StripANSI(s string) string {
+ if !strings.ContainsRune(s, 0x1b) {
+ return s
+ }
+ return ansiEscape.ReplaceAllString(s, "")
+ }
+

58		}

61		}
